| *** WARNING ***                                                                                                                                                                                                                          |
| The block and item IDs are dynamic and will be different on each world!                                                                                                                                                                  |
| DO NOT use them for anything "proper"!! (other than manual editing/fixing of raw world data or something)                                                                                                                                |
| *** ALSO ***                                                                                                                                                                                                                             |
| The server doesn't have a list of sub block and sub items                                                                                                                                                                                |
| (= items with different damage value or blocks with different metadata).                                                                                                                                                                 |
| That is why the block and item list dumps only contain one entry per block/item class (separate ID) when run on a server.                                                                                                                |
